> git rev-parse --symbolic-full-name sam-test@{u}
> git rev-list --left-right sam-test...refs/remotes/origin/sam-test
> git for-each-ref --sort -committerdate --format %(refname) %(objectname) %(*objectname)
> git remote --verbose

> git rev-list --left-right test-run...refs/remotes/origin/test-run

> git rev-list --left-right test-run...refs/remotes/origin/test-run
> git for-each-ref --sort -committerdate --format %(refname) %(objectname) %(*objectname)
> git remote --verbose
> git config --get commit.template
> git status -z -u

> git rev-parse --symbolic-full-name test-run@{u}
> git rev-list --left-right test-run...refs/remotes/origin/test-run

> git rev-list --left-right test-run...refs/remotes/origin/test-run
> git for-each-ref --sort -committerdate --format %(refname) %(objectname) %(*objectname)
> git remote --verbose
> git config --get commit.template
> git status -z -u
